! Numerals
! ========

! The initial lexica
! ------------------

LEXICON Numeral
 MILJON ;           ! a noun of its own
 UNDERDUHAT ;       ! for generator under 1000
 JUSTDUHAT ;        ! going via 1000
 OVERDUHAT ;     ! for generator over 1000
 OLD ;           ! for "thirteen hundred, etc.
num-imprecise ;
num-collective ;
 +Use/Circ: ARABIC ;          ! for the arabic numerals        !
 +Use/Circ: ROMAN ;           ! for the roman numerals         !
 +Use/Circ: NUM-PREFIXES ;    ! for §34 etc.                   !
 +Use/Circ: ISOLATED-NUMEXP ; ! for ½ etc.                     !
11TO99F ;
21TO99 ;
DUHAT ;
1TO9DUHAT ;
O-NUPPELOHKAI ;
NUPPELOHKAICUODI ;
NUPPELOHKAI ;



! We now run through the alphabetic numerals, ending up with the case
! inflection of the final number.

! Million, a noun of its own
! --------------------------

LEXICON MILJON
miljovdna+v4+Num+Sg+Nom:miljon%> K ;                !Num or N?
miljovdna+Num+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub:miljun%> K ;                         !
miljovdna+v1:miljovdna OKTA ;
miljovdna+v2:millijovdna OKTA ;
miljovdna+v3:millijuvdna OKTA ;
miljovnnat+A+Ord:miljovnnag VUOSTTAS ;    ! This should NOT be N, since it is the starting point of the Ordinal
miljovnnat+A+Ord:millijovnnag VUOSTTAS ;
miljovnnat+A+Ord:miljonag VUOSTTAS ;
miljárda:miljár'da OKTA ;         !Num or N?
miljárddat+A+Ord:miljárddag VUOSTTAS ;



! Overduhat, for the numerals over 1000
! --------------------------------------

LEXICON OVERDUHAT
O-OKTAF ;
O-2TO9F ;
 O-JUSTLOGIF ; ! 10000
 O-2TO9LOG ;   ! 20000, 30000, ...
 O-NUPPELOT ;  ! 11000, 12000, ...
 O-CUODI ;     ! 100000
 O-2TO9CUO ;   ! 200000, 300000, ...

! All the child lexica of OVERDUHAT have the prefix O-.
! They are directed via their respective numerals to the lexicon JUSTDUHAT.


! Thousands

LEXICON O-OKTAF
okta:okta# JUSTDUHAT ;
akta:akta# JUSTDUHAT ;
JUSTDUHAT ;
DUHAT ;


LEXICON O-2TO9F
guokte:guokte#   JUSTDUHAT ;
golbma:golbma#   JUSTDUHAT ;
njeallje:njeallje# JUSTDUHAT ;
njeallj:njeallja# JUSTDUHAT ;
vihtta:vihtta#   JUSTDUHAT ;
guhtta:guhtta#   JUSTDUHAT ;
čieža:čieža#    JUSTDUHAT ;
čieža+Use/Sub:gieža#    JUSTDUHAT ;
gávcci:gávcci#   JUSTDUHAT ;
ovcci:ovcci#    JUSTDUHAT ;

LEXICON 1TO9DUHAT
oktaduhát:ok'ta OKTADUHAT ;
guokteduhát:guok't GUOKTEDUHAT ;
nubbeduhát:nubb NUBBEDUHAT ;
golbmaduhát:golbma GOLBMADUHAT ;
njealljeduhát:njeallj GUOKTEDUHAT ;
njealljaduhát+Num+Sg+Nom:njeallja#duhát%> K ;
njealljaduhát+Num+Sg+Acc:njeallja#duhát%> K ;
njealljaduhát+Num+Sg+Gen:njealja#duhát%> K ;
njealljaduhát+Num+Sg+Acc:njeallja#duháh%>a K ;
njealljaduhát+Num+Sg+Gen:njealja#duháh%>a K ;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     vihttaduhát:vi VIHTTADUHAT ;
guhttaduhát:gu VIHTTADUHAT ;
čiežaduhát:či CIEZADUHAT ;
giežaduhát:gi CIEZADUHAT ;
gávcciduhát:gák'ci GAVCCIDUHAT ;
ovcciduhát:ok'ci GAVCCIDUHAT ;

! Underduhat, the numerals under 1000
! -----------------------------------


LEXICON UNDERDUHAT
OKTAF ;     ! 1, 11
2TO9F ;     ! 2-9
BARELOGIF ;     ! 10
2TO9LOG ; ! 20-90
CUODI ;     ! 100
2TO9CUO ; ! 200-999
1TO9CUODI ;
LOHKI ;
NUPPELOGIS ;

LEXICON OKTAF
num-ordinal-1 ;
okta:ok'ta OKTA ;
okta#lohki:ok'ta OKTALOHKI ;
akta+Num+Sg+Nom:akta%> K ;
akta#lohki+Num+Sg+Nom:akta#lohki%> K ;
! K ; this lead to "go +Clt" as an analysis, and was removed.
! Thus, direction to K should be made at an earlier point


LEXICON 2TO9F
num-ordinal-2to9 ; ! also ordinals of complex numbers
guokte:guok't GUOKTE ;
guovttis+N+Coll+Sg+Nom+Use/NG:guovttes%> K ;
guovttis:guo GUOVTTIS ;
golbma GOLBMA ;
golmmas:golbmas OVCCIS ;
njeallje:njeallj GUOKTE ;
njeallja+Num+Sg+Nom:njeallja%> K ;
njeallja+Num+Sg+Gen:njealja%> K ;
njeallja+Num+Sg+Acc:njealja%> K ;
njealjis:njealljis OVCCIS ;
vihtta:vi VIHTTA ;
viđas:vi VIDAS ;
guhtta:gu VIHTTA ;
guđas:gu VIDAS ;
čieža:či CIEZA ;
gieža:gi CIEZA ;
čiežas:čieh'čas OVCCIS ;
giežas:gieh'čas OVCCIS ;
gávcci:gák'ci GAVCCI ;
gávccis:gák'cis OVCCIS ;
ovcci:ok'ci GAVCCI ;
ovccis:ok'cis OVCCIS ;


LEXICON 11TO99F
okta#nuppe#lohkái:ok'ta OKTANUPPELOHKAI ;
okta#nuppe#lohkái+Num+Sg+Loc:okta%>#nuppe#logi%>s K ; !time
okta#nuppe#lohkái+Num+Sg+Ill:okta%>#nuppe#lohká%>j K ; !time
okta#nuppe#lohkái+Num+Sg+Attr:okta%>#nuppe#logi%> K ; !time
okta#goalmmát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTAGOALMMATLOHKAI ;
okta#njealját#lohkái:ok'ta OKTANJEALJATLOHKAI ;
okta#viđát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTAVIDATLOHKAI ;
okta#guđát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTAGUDATLOHKAI ;
okta#čihččet#lohkái:ok'ta OKTACIHCCETLOHKAI ;
okta#gávccát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTAGAVCCATLOHKAI ;
okta#ovccát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTAOVCCATLOHKAI ;
okta#logát#lohkái:ok'ta OKTALOGATLOHKAI ;

! Arabic numerals
! ---------------


LEXICON NUM-PREFIXES 
 §+Use/Circ:§       ARABIC ; ! §24
 §§+Use/Circ:§§     ARABIC ; ! §§24
 §% +Use/Circ:§%    ARABIC ; ! § 24
 §§% +Use/Circ:§§%  ARABIC ; ! §§ 24
 %-+Use/Circ:%- ARABIC ; ! -24
 %‒+Use/Circ:%‒ ARABIC ; ! -24 U+2012
 %–+Use/Circ:%– ARABIC ; ! -24 U+2013
 %—+Use/Circ:%— ARABIC ; ! -24 U+2014
 %―+Use/Circ:%― ARABIC ; ! -24 U+2015
 %++Use/Circ:%+ ARABIC ; ! <plus>24
 %-% +Use/Circ:%-%  ARABIC ; ! - 24
 %‒% +Use/Circ:%‒%  ARABIC ; ! - 24 U+2012
 %–% +Use/Circ:%–%  ARABIC ; ! - 24 U+2013
 %—% +Use/Circ:%—%  ARABIC ; ! - 24 U+2014
 %―% +Use/Circ:%―%  ARABIC ; ! - 24 U+2015
 %+% +Use/Circ:%+%  ARABIC ; ! <plus> 24
 %*+Use/Circ:%* ARABIC ; ! *24
 %$+Use/Circ:%$ ARABIC ; ! $24
 %€+Use/Circ:%€ ARABIC ; ! €24
 %<+Use/Circ:%[%<%] ARABIC ; ! <24
 %>+Use/Circ:%[%>%] ARABIC ; ! >24
 s%.+Use/Circ:s%. ARABIC ; ! s.24

LEXICON ARABIC
< [1|2|3|4|5|6|7|8|9|%0] > ARABICLOOP ;
< [1|2|3|4|5|6|7|8|9|%0] > ARABICLOOPORD ;
< [1|2|3|4|5|6|7|8|9|%0] > ARABICLOOPCOLL ;

LEXICON ARABICLOOP
 +Use/Circ: ARABIC ;
 %-+Use/Circ:%- ARABIC ; ! 1-2 multipart numbers 
 %–+Use/Circ:%– ARABIC ; ! 1–2 multipart numbers 
 %—+Use/Circ:%— ARABIC ; ! 1—2 multipart numbers 
 %.%-+Use/Circ:%.%- ARABIC ; ! 1.-2 multipart numbers ! !
 %.%–+Use/Circ:%.%– ARABIC ; ! 1.–2 multipart numbers ! !
 %.%—+Use/Circ:%.%— ARABIC ; ! 1.—2 multipart numbers ! !
 %-% +Use/Circ:%-%  ARABIC ; ! 1- 2 multipart numbers 
 %–% +Use/Circ:%–%  ARABIC ; ! 1– 2 multipart numbers 
 %—% +Use/Circ:%—%  ARABIC ; ! 1— 2 multipart numbers 
 % %-+Use/Circ:% %- ARABIC ; ! 1 -2 multipart numbers 
 % %–+Use/Circ:% %– ARABIC ; ! 1 –2 multipart numbers 
 % %—+Use/Circ:% %— ARABIC ; ! 1 —2 multipart numbers 
 % %-% +Use/Circ:% %-%  ARABIC ; ! 1 - 2 multipart numbers 
 % %–% +Use/Circ:% %–%  ARABIC ; ! 1 – 2 multipart numbers 
 % %—% +Use/Circ:% %—%  ARABIC ; ! 1 — 2 multipart numbers 
 % %-%-% +Use/Circ:% %-%-%  ARABIC ; ! 1 -- 2 multipart numbers 
 % %–%–% +Use/Circ:% %–%–%  ARABIC ; ! 1 –– 2 multipart numbers 
 % %—%—% +Use/Circ:% %—%—%  ARABIC ; ! 1 —— 2 multipart numbers 
 %.+Use/Circ:%. ARABIC ; 
 %:+Use/Circ:%: ARABIC ; 
 %,+Use/Circ:%, ARABIC ; 
 % +Use/Circ:%  ARABIC ; ! Allowing for "23 500". 
   +Use/Circ:  ARABIC ; ! Allowing for "23 500" w/nbsp (init char = alt-space)
 %/+Use/Circ:%/ ARABIC ; ! 24/12
 %/% +Use/Circ:%/%  ARABIC ; ! 24/ 12
 % %/+Use/Circ:% %/ ARABIC ; ! 24 /12
 '+Use/Circ:'7 ARABIC ; ! Since ' denotes cons.grad. This is not optimal either.
 
 +Num+Use/Circ: RHyph ; ! Number compounds, with hyphen
 +Num+Use/Circ: RHyph ; ! Hyphen also when other than arabic have not
 
 ,%-+Num+Use/Circ:,%- ARABICCASES ; ! 10,-
 ,%-+Num+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:.%- ARABICCASES ; ! 10.- It is wrong, but written.
 
  % %-+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:% %- ARABICDELIMITER; ! 1 - multipart numbers - "1 - :s"?
  % %-%-+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:% %-%- ARABICDELIMITER; ! 1 -- multipart numbers
  %%+Num+Nom+Use/Circ:%%  ARABICDELIMITER ; ! 50%. It is wrong, but 75 % of us write "75%".
  % %%+Num+Nom+Use/Circ:% %%  ARABICDELIMITER ; ! the correct ones as well... 50 % etc.
  ARABICDELIMITER ; ! list of number-case delimiters

LEXICON ARABICLOOPORD
 +A+Ord:%. # ;
 +A+Ord+Use/Circ: ARABICDELIMITERORD ;
 < [a|b|c|d|e|f|f% f] > ACASETAG ;

LEXICON ACASETAG  ! 1e+Num+Sg+Num:1e
+Num: ARABICCASES ;

LEXICON ARABICLOOPCOLL
 +N+Coll+Use/Circ: ARABICDELIMITERCOLL ;


LEXICON ARABICDELIMITER ! blank + 3 delim, what does the lg counc prefer?
 +Num:           ARABICCASE0 ; ! This is the 1984 case, ie NGA
 +Num:%:         ARABICCASE  ; ! This is the 1984:s case.
 +Num+Use/Sub:   ARABICCASE  ; ! This is the 1984s case.
 +Num+Use/Sub:'7 ARABICCASE  ; ! This is the 1984's case. 
 +Num+Use/Sub:’  ARABICCASE  ; ! optio-B07 = ’
 +Num+Use/Sub:%- ARABICCASE  ; ! This is the 1984-s case. 
 +Num+Use/Sub:%- NUMERALCOMPOUNDS ; ! 6-jáhkasaš 
 +Num+Use/Sub:´  ARABICCASE  ; ! This is the 1984´s case.


LEXICON ARABICDELIMITERORD
!            ARABICCASE0   ; ! This is the 1984 case, ie NGA
 :%:         ARABICCASEORD ; ! This is the 1984:s case.
 +Use/Sub:   ARABICCASEORD ; ! This is the 1984s case. 
 +Use/Sub:'7 ARABICCASEORD ; ! This is the 1984's case. 
 +Use/Sub:%- ARABICCASEORD ; ! This is the 1984-s case. 

LEXICON ARABICDELIMITERCOLL
!            ARABICCASE0    ; ! This is the 1984 case, ie NGA
 :%:         ARABICCASECOLL ; ! This is the 1984:s case. 
 +Use/Sub:   ARABICCASECOLL ; ! This is the 1984s case. 
 +Use/Sub:'7 ARABICCASECOLL ; ! This is the 1984's case. 
 +Use/Sub:%- ARABICCASECOLL ; ! This is the 1984-s case. 

LEXICON ARABICCASES ! to distinguish between 0 and oblique
ARABICCASE0 ;
ARABICCASE ;

LEXICON ARABICCASE0
 +Sg+Nom: # ;
 +Sg+Gen: # ;
 +Sg+Acc: # ;


LEXICON ARABICCASE
!   +Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:   # ;
!     f+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:f  # ; ! s. 123f.
!    ff+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:ff # ; ! s. 123ff.
!  b+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:b  # ; ! § 123b
!  c+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:c  # ; ! § 123c
!  d+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:d  # ; ! § 123d
!  e+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:e  # ; ! § 123e
!  š+Sg+Nom+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:š  # ;

! +Sg+Gen+Use/Sub:      # ; 
! +Sg+Acc+Use/Sub:      # ; 
 +Sg+Gen+Use/Sub:a     # ; ! But here 123a 123
 +Sg+Acc+Use/Sub:a     # ; 
 +Sg+Gen+Use/Sub:ža    # ; 
 +Sg+Acc+Use/Sub:ža    # ; 
 +Sg+Ill+Use/NG:%>i    # ;
 +Sg+Ill+Use/Sub:ij    # ;
 +Sg+Ill+Use/Sub:žij   # ; 
 +Sg+Ill+Use/Sub:áj    # ; ! Testing over the weekend. !
 +Sg+Loc:%>s           K ;
 +Sg+Loc+Use/Sub:is    K ;
 +Sg+Loc+Use/Sub:žis   K ;
 +Sg+Loc+Use/Sub:as    # ;
 +Sg+Com:%>in          # ;
 +Sg+Com+Use/Sub:žijn  # ;
 +Sg+Com+Use/Sub:ain   # ;
 +Sg+Ess:%>n           # ;
 +Sg+Ess+Use/Sub:žin   # ;
 +Sg+Ess+Use/Sub:an    # ;
 +Pl+Nom:%>t           K ;
 +Pl+Gen+Use/Sub:ijd9  K ;
 +Pl+Gen+Use/NG:%>id9  K ;
 +Pl+Acc+Use/Sub:ijd9  K ;
 +Pl+Acc+Use/NG:%>id9  K ;
 +Pl+Ill+Use/Sub:ijde  K ; ! 100:iide čuđiide
 +Pl+Ill+Use/Sub:ijdda K ; ! 1000:idda duháhiidda
 +Pl+Ill+Use/NG:%>ide  K ; ! 100:iide čuđiide
 +Pl+Ill+Use/Sub:idda  K ; ! 1000:idda duháhiidda
 +Pl+Loc:%>in          K ;
 +Pl+Com:%>igujn       K ;
 
 LEXICON ARABICCASEORD
 +Sg+Gen:%>da     K ;
 +Sg+Acc:%>da     K ;
 +Sg+Ill:%>dij    K ;
 +Sg+Loc:%>dis    K ;
 +Sg+Com:%>dijn   K ;
 +Sg+Ess:%>din    K ;
 +Pl+Nom:%>dat    K ;
 +Pl+Gen:%>dijd9  K ;
 +Pl+Acc:%>dijd9  K ;
 +Pl+Ill:%>dijdda K ;
 +Pl+Loc:%>dijn   K ;
 +Pl+Com:%>digujn K ;
 
 LEXICON ARABICCASECOLL
 +Sg+Gen:%>sa   K ;
 +Sg+Acc:%>sa   K ;
 +Sg+Ill:%>sij  K ;
 +Sg+Loc:%>sis  K ;
 +Sg+Com:%>sijn K ;


! The Roman numerals !
! ------------------ !

LEXICON ROMAN !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROM-THOUSAND ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-HUNDRED ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-TEN ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-ONE ; !

LEXICON ROM-THOUSAND !^C^
 M+Use/Circ:M ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MM+Use/Circ:MM ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMM+Use/Circ:MMM ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMMM+Use/Circ:MMMM ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMMMM+Use/Circ:MMMMM ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !

LEXICON ROM-THOUSAND-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-HUNDRED ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-TEN ;				!
 +Use/Circ: ROM-ONE ;				!
 +Use/Circ: ROM-SPLIT ; !

LEXICON ROM-HUNDRED !^C^
 C+Use/Circ:C ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CC+Use/Circ:CC ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CCC+Use/Circ:CCC ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CD+Use/Circ:CD ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 D+Use/Circ:D ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DC+Use/Circ:DC ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DCC+Use/Circ:DCC ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DCCC+Use/Circ:DCCC ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CM+Use/Circ:CM ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !

LEXICON ROM-HUNDRED-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-TEN ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-ONE ;				!
 +Use/Circ: ROM-SPLIT ; !

LEXICON ROM-TEN !^C^
 X+Use/Circ:X ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XX+Use/Circ:XX ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XXX+Use/Circ:XXX ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XL+Use/Circ:XL ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 L+Use/Circ:L ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LX+Use/Circ:LX ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LXX+Use/Circ:LXX ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LXXX+Use/Circ:LXXX ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XC+Use/Circ:XC ROM-TEN-TAG; !

LEXICON ROM-TEN-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-ONE ; !
 +Use/Circ: ROM-SPLIT ; !

LEXICON ROM-ONE !^C^
 I+Use/Circ:I ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 II+Use/Circ:II ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 III+Use/Circ:III ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 IV+Use/Circ:IV ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 V+Use/Circ:V ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VI+Use/Circ:VI ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VII+Use/Circ:VII ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VIII+Use/Circ:VIII ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 IX+Use/Circ:IX ROM-ONE-TAG; !

LEXICON ROM-ONE-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
! +N: ROMNUMTAG ; !^C^ !The Olav viđeš fix (Roman V now gets A)
 +Use/Circ: ROM-SPLIT ; !

! Here, we split the Roman numerals, in order to account for cases like "Kapihtal II-IV".
! We may send this first part directly to ROM-TAG below (and get the +Num tag), or we may
! send them through a second loop, identical to the first one, but marked wit "2" (the lexica
! are called 2ROMAN, etc. We do this instead of making a loop, since we do not want cases
! like "II-IV-VI-VII-IX". If that should turn out to be a good idea, a loop would do the
! trick.

LEXICON ROM-SPLIT !^C^
 +Use/Circ:%- 2ROMAN ; ! II-VI, etc. !


! Here goes loop 2.

LEXICON 2ROMAN !^C^
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-THOUSAND ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-HUNDRED ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-TEN ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-ONE ; !

LEXICON 2ROM-THOUSAND !^C^
 M+Use/Circ:M 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MM+Use/Circ:MM 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMM+Use/Circ:MMM 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMMM+Use/Circ:MMMM 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !
 MMMMM+Use/Circ:MMMMM 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG; !

LEXICON 2ROM-THOUSAND-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-HUNDRED ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-TEN ;				 !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-ONE ;				!

LEXICON 2ROM-HUNDRED !^C^
 C+Use/Circ:C 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CC+Use/Circ:CC 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CCC+Use/Circ:CCC 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CD+Use/Circ:CD 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 D+Use/Circ:D 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DC+Use/Circ:DC 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DCC+Use/Circ:DCC 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 DCCC+Use/Circ:DCCC 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !
 CM+Use/Circ:CM 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG; !

LEXICON 2ROM-HUNDRED-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-TEN ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-ONE ;				!
LEXICON 2ROM-TEN !^C^
 X+Use/Circ:X 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XX+Use/Circ:XX 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XXX+Use/Circ:XXX 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XL+Use/Circ:XL 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 L+Use/Circ:L 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LX+Use/Circ:LX 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LXX+Use/Circ:LXX 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 LXXX+Use/Circ:LXXX 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !
 XC+Use/Circ:XC 2ROM-TEN-TAG; !

LEXICON 2ROM-TEN-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !
 +Use/Circ: 2ROM-ONE ; !

LEXICON 2ROM-ONE !^C^
 I+Use/Circ:I 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 II+Use/Circ:II 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 III+Use/Circ:III 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 IV+Use/Circ:IV 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 V+Use/Circ:V 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VI+Use/Circ:VI 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VII+Use/Circ:VII 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 VIII+Use/Circ:VIII 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !
 IX+Use/Circ:IX 2ROM-ONE-TAG; !

LEXICON 2ROM-ONE-TAG !^C^
 +Use/Circ: ROMNUMTAG ; !

LEXICON ROMNUMTAG
 +Num+Nom+Use/Circ:%> # ; !
 +Num+Gen+Use/Circ:%> # ; !
 +Num+Acc+Use/Circ:%> # ; !
 +A+Ord+Use/Circ:%.%> # ; ! !III. as ordinal.
 +A+Ord+Use/Circ:%> # ; ! !Looking for trouble...
 +Num+Use/Circ:%: ROMNUMTAGOBL ; !
 +Num+Use/Circ:'7 ROMNUMTAGOBL ; !
 +Num+Use/Circ:%- ROMNUMTAGOBL ; !
 +Num+Use/Circ:%´ ROMNUMTAGOBL ; !
! +Num: ROMNUMTAGOBL ; !^C^

LEXICON ROMNUMTAGOBL !^C^
 +Gen+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:%>a # ; ! ! But here 123a 123
 +Acc+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:%>a # ; ! !
 +Ill+Use/Circ:%>i # ; ! 
 +Ill+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:%>ij # ; ! !
 +Ill+Use/Sub+Use/Circ:%>áj # ; ! !
 +Loc+Use/Circ:%>s # ; !
 +Com+Use/Circ:%>in # ; !
 +Ess+Use/Circ:%>n # ; !


! A final section with some isolated numeral expresssions !
! ------------------------------------------------------- !

LEXICON ISOLATED-NUMEXP
 ½+Num:½ # ;
 ¹+Num:¹ # ;
 ²+Num:² # ;
 ³+Num:³ # ;
 ¼+Num:¼ # ;
 ¾+Num:¾ # ;
